<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>FG NEXUS ANNOUNCES THIRD QUARTER HIGHLIGHTS AND SHAREHOLDER UPDATE</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Charlotte,
NC &ndash; November 20, 2025 &ndash; FG Nexus (Nasdaq: FGNX, FGNXP) </B>(the &ldquo;Company&rdquo; or &ldquo;FG Nexus&rdquo;), today
provided key highlights for the period ended September 30, 2025.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Subsequent
Updates</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">On
October 23, 2025, the Company commenced repurchasing its common shares under its previously announced share buyback program. To support
this activity, the Company borrowed approximately $10 million and sold 10,922 ETH, with proceeds being deployed to accelerate repurchases
and enhance shareholder value.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">To
date, these actions have resulted in the repurchase of 3.4 million common shares at an average price of approximately $3.45 per share.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">As
of November 19, 2025, the Company holds 40,005 ETH and cash and USDC holdings of approximately $37 million. Total debt outstanding is
$11.9 million, common shares outstanding are 40.1 million (including 1.3 million unconverted prefunded warrants), and net asset value
per share is approximately $3.94. Refer to the Company&rsquo;s website and ETH tacker at <U>https://fgnexus.io/eth-treasury-tracker/</U>
for additional information.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;Since
commencing the buyback, we have repurchased 8% of our shares outstanding at a substantial discount to our net asset value while maintaining
a strong ETH and cash balance,&rdquo; said Kyle Cerminara, Chairman &amp; CEO of FG Nexus. &ldquo;We plan to continue buying back shares
while our stock trades below NAV, which creates increasingly asymptotic effect on our per-share valuation metrics as the number of shares
outstanding declines and net asset value per share increases.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>About
FG Nexus</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">FG
Nexus (Nasdaq: FGNX, FGNXP) (the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;) is focused on building a digital asset treasury and a leading platform for the
tokenization of real-world assets. To enhance the yield on its treasury, the Company will stake its ETH and implement additional yield
strategies while positioning itself as a strategic gateway into digital-asset-powered finance, including tokenized RWAs and stablecoin-based
yield solutions. The FGNX<SUP>&reg; </SUP>logo is a registered trademark.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
